3531<h1>

353210 Cabinet Organization Ideas + How to Organize Your Kitchen Cabinets in 3 Steps</h1>

3533

3534</div>

3535</div>

3536</div>

3537</div>

3538<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-fcc-ad--be-cffdaa">

3539<div>

3540<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3541<div>

3542<h6>

3543By Mikael Short &amp; the Vevano Home Team</h6>

3544

3545

3546<h6>

3547June 16, 2021</h6>

3548

3549</div>

3550</div>

3551</div>

3552</div>

3553</div>

3554</div>

3564<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-dce-baa-ef-ac-fabe">

3565<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

3566<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

3567<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

3568<div class="">

3569<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-ceaf-de-e-aaf-ce">

3570<div class="merce-column-container">

3572<div>

3573<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3574<div>

3575<p>

3576Knowing how to organize your kitchen cabinets can add both practicality and style to the main activity hub of your home. Organizing your cabinets keeps your kitchen supplies and materials handy when you need them while also optimizing the storage available to you. It&rsquo;s all about making your kitchen storage space work for you.</p>

3577

3578

3579<p>

3580It&rsquo;s easier than ever to truly customize your kitchen cabinets, thanks to a variety of styles and options of cabinet and drawer organization tools available. Taking your cabinet organization to the next level will ensure a clutter-free zone for cooking and hosting.</p>

3581

3582

3583<p>

3584Kitchen cabinet organization will ultimately boil down to what will most help you in the kitchen, where, and when. Give every item in your kitchen a place to live, and you&rsquo;ll always know where to find it and where to put it when you&rsquo;re done.</p>

3585

3586

3587<p>

3588Whether you have many <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-kitchen/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20organization">

3589kitchen cabinets</a>

3590 or a tight-and-mighty few, there are ways to optimize and organize the storage space in your cupboards so it supports your activities in the kitchen.</p>

3591

3592</div>

3593</div>

3594</div>

3595</div>

3596</div>

3597</div>

3598</div>

3599</div>

3600</div>

3617<div>

3618<h2>

3619Kitchen Drawer &amp; Cabinet Organization Ideas</h2>

3620

3621

3622<p>

3623You don&rsquo;t need to have built-in features to create custom cabinets or drawers for your kitchen. Drawer and cabinet organizers come in different sizes and styles to assist you in organizing your existing cabinets and drawers. If you need help figuring out what will fit your cabinets to optimize the space, <a href="https://design.vevano.com/design-services/">

3624reach out to our designers</a>

3625 and they can get you set up with the right kitchen cabinet accessories.</p>

3626

3652<div>

3653<h3>

3654Lazy Susans</h3>

3655

3656</div>

3657</div>

3658</div>

3659</div>

3660<div class="">

3661<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-f--ab-be-adec">

3662<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-f--ab-be-adec">

3663<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

3664<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

3665<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

3666<div class="">

3667<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-bab--faa-ac-ecfab">

3668<div class="merce-column-container">

3669<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE--ce-fa--dfaae">

3670<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf -ce-fa--dfaae-singleImageAlignment">

3671<img class="-ce-fa--dfaae-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/MVXv1_N9-0u6JmlkP5_yy6uVTmaM_ntCv0Xbkb97XPE/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL0Jsb2clMjBQb3N0cy9DYWJpbmV0JTIwT3JnYW5pemF0aW9uJTIwSWRlYXMlMjBhbmQlMjBLaXRjaGVuJTIwQ2FiaW5ldHMvNzA1Ny0yLmpwZw" alt="lazy susan revAShelf" title="lazy susan revAShelf"/>

3672</div>

3673</div>

3674<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-aae-cfb---bceeacc">

3675<div>

3676<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3677<div>

3678<p>

3679<strong>

3680Lazy Susans</strong>

3681 are the corner cabinet&rsquo;s best friend. The swivel shelf is ideal where it may be an awkward fitting cabinet that&rsquo;s hard to access. Just a turn of the Lazy Susan and items in the back come to the front for easy grabbing! Lazy Susans work great for storing pots, pans, Tupperware (be sure to pair the lids and containers together), or even snacks or easy-to-access food. They are also super easy to clean when you pop out the spinning shelves, so Lazy Susans are also nice for food items that might be prone to spilling.</p>

There are also <a href="https://vevano.com/product/7011-432-bfbbsc-6c-432-series-natural-maple-between-cabinet-pull-out-organizer-with-ball-bearing-soft-close-6-x-23-x-30/">

4941<h3>

4942Floating Shelves</h3>

4943

4944</div>

4945</div>

4946</div>

4947</div>

4948<div class="">

4949<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-ccbaef-bd-d-ed-fcbbf">

4950<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-ccbaef-bd-d-ed-fcbbf">

4951<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

4952<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

4953<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4954<div class="">

4955<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-faaf-dd-cb-fa-fd">

4956<div class="merce-column-container">

4957<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-fec-e-b-c-bce">

4958<div>

4959<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4960<div>

4961<p>

4962<strong>

4963Floating shelves</strong>

4964 that are not contained in cabinets can add additional storage while creating variety in your design&mdash;providing a home for your commonly used items, such as bowls, mugs, etc. These work great when placed at eye level.</p>

4965

5001<h3>

5002Kitchen Racks and Hooks</h3>

5003

5004</div>

5005</div>

5006</div>

5007</div>

5008<div class="">

5009<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-dfba-ea-a-aca-fcfdfd">

5011<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

5012<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

5026<p>

5027Whether within or outside your cabinets, you can further optimize your organization system in your kitchen with hooks or racks to hold various items. A <strong>

5028pot or pan rack</strong>

5029, hanging or mounted near the stove, can make a statement as decor while also providing an easily accessible storage place for small to moderately sized cookware.</p>

5030

5031

5032<p>

5033Similarly, a <strong>

5034wine or stemware rack</strong>

5035 attached underneath a cabinet provides an attractive storage solution for your glassware.</p>

5036

5037

5038<p>

5039A <strong>

5040towel rack attachment</strong>

5041 on the cabinet door beneath the sink may also come in handy.</p>

5042

5131<div>

5132<h2>

5133How to Organize Your Kitchen Cabinets and Drawers</h2>

5134

5135</div>

5136</div>

5137</div>

5138</div>

5139<div class="">

5140<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-ad-be-f-b-cfcbf">

5141<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-ad-be-f-b-cfcbf">

5142<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

5143<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

5144<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

5145<div class="">

5146<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-eed-f-b-bda-fda">

5147<div class="merce-column-container">

5148<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-bbeec-e-aeb-bba-bfddc">

5149<div>

5150<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

5151<div>

5152<h3>

51531. Empty and Clean Cabinets and Drawers</h3>

5154

5155

5156<p>

5157If you want to start completely fresh, then it&rsquo;s a good idea to take everything out of your kitchen cabinets and drawers to see what you have&hellip; and to also clean the cabinets before putting everything back in.</p>

5158

5159

5160<p>

5161For this first step, remove items from your cabinets and drawers and wipe down the interior surfaces, replacing (or adding) any shelving paper where necessary to provide a clean and ready cabinet.</p>

5162

5163

5164<p>

5165While they&rsquo;re empty, consider measuring your kitchen cabinets and drawers. That way, you have a better idea of how much space you have available for storage and you can buy the proper sizes for any kitchen organizers you may want to add in the future.</p>

5166

5167</div>

5168</div>

5169</div>

5170</div>

5171<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-adbd-fef-c-bf-abfbf">

5172<div>

5173<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

5174<div>

5175<h3>

51762. Discard Unused Items</h3>

5177

5178

5179<p>

5180To create space for better organization and make room for anything new you may need, consider tossing anything you haven&rsquo;t used in more than a year or two.</p>

5181

5182

5183<p>

5184Donate, recycle, or discard glass jars, utensils, dishware, storage containers, and other kitchen items that you don&rsquo;t use regularly. With a bit of creativity, you can repurpose some unused items, like turning Tupperware that doesn&rsquo;t have a matching lid into a drawer organizer if the size is right!</p>

5185

5186</div>

5187</div>

5188</div>

5189</div>

5190<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-bdbb-fb-cce-ad-cbff">

5191<div>

5192<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

5193<div>

5194<h3>

51953. Organize Your Kitchen By Category, Section, or Zone</h3>

5196

5197

5198<p>

5199The kitchen is a hub for so many activities that it&rsquo;s helpful to have materials and tools that serve a similar purpose in coordinating areas. After cleaning everything out of your cupboards and discarding unused items, organize your kitchen supplies into groups that you can place strategically throughout your <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/kitchen-layout-ideas/" target="_blank">

5200kitchen layout</a>

5201.</p>

5202

5203

5204<p>

5205From there, you can map out where you want each category of items to live in your kitchen.</p>

5206

5207

5208<p>

5209For example, your cooking utensils, pots, pans, etc., can live in the base cabinets surrounding your stove. And your dishware and glassware might fit great in the cabinets above your kitchen sink or dishwasher so you can conveniently put them away after washing. If you have an island with seating or near seating, island drawers would be handy for flatware, placemats, or other dining accouterments.</p>

5210

5211</div>

5212</div>

5213</div>

5214</div>

5215<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-bab--a--dfdec">

5216<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf bab--a--dfdec-singleImageAlignment">

5217<img class="bab--a--dfdec-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/wT1N4d6ddVxwkZOAccylNz2STqo1YOuL4QlK_FgPbRk/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL0Jsb2clMjBQb3N0cy9DYWJpbmV0JTIwT3JnYW5pemF0aW9uJTIwSWRlYXMlMjBhbmQlMjBLaXRjaGVuJTIwQ2FiaW5ldHMvNDA2NjgtMi5qcGc" alt="Rev-a-Shelf Chrome Pull-out Organizer" title="Rev-a-Shelf Chrome Pull-out Organizer"/>

5218</div>

5219</div>

5220<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-add--f-a-ffba">

5221<div>

5222<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

5223<div>

5224<p style="text-align: center;">

5225<a href="https://vevano.com/product/40668-5cw2-1222-cr-5cw2-series-chrome-pull-out-organizer-1175-x-22-x-18/">

5226<em>

5227Rev-a-Shelf Chrome Pull-out Organizer</em>

5228</a>

5229</p>

5230

5231</div>

5232</div>

5233</div>

5234</div>

5235<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-d-e---aadbcdcb">

5236<div>

5237<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

5238<div>

5239<p>

5240If organizing your whole kitchen feels overwhelming, try paring down to cleaning and organizing one category (or zone) at a time so you&rsquo;re not trying to organize everything all at once.</p>

5241

5242

5243<p>

5244Potential zones or categories to plan for in your kitchen cabinets:</p>

5245

5246

5247<ul>

5248

5249 <li>

5250Prep - knives, cutting boards, measuring cups and spoons, colanders, etc.</li>

5251

5252 <li>

5253Oven or stovetop cooking - pots, pans, stirring utensils, etc.</li>

5254

5255 <li>

5256Dishes and glassware</li>

5257

5258 <li>

5259Sink storage - cleaning supplies, cloth, paper towels, etc.</li>

5260

5261 <li>

5262Food or pantry storage</li>

5263

5264 <li>

5265Small appliances - mixers, blenders, toasters, coffee/tea makers, etc.</li>

5266

5267 <li>

5268Storage items - plastic bags, foil, Tupperware, jars, etc.</li>

5269

5270 <li>

5271Catch-all drawers - affectionately called &ldquo;junk drawers&rdquo;</li>

5272

5273</ul>

5274

5275

5276<p>

5277Consider installing drawer and cabinet organizational attachments or inserts that can help you to make the most of your cabinet space.</p>

5278

5279</div>

5280</div>

5281</div>

5282</div>

5283</div>

5284</div>

5285</div>

5286</div>

5287</div>

5288</div>

5289</div>

5290</div>

5291</div>

5292</div>

5293</div>

5294</div>

5295</div>

5296</div>

5297</div>

5298</div>

5299</div>

5300</div>

5301<div class="">

5302<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-c-e--ec-feadbb">

5303<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-c-e--ec-feadbb">

5304<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

5305<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

5306<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

5307<div class="">

5308<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-acbbe--e-abaf-adbcb">

5309<div class="merce-column-container">

5310<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK---c-aa-eed">

5311<div>

5312<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

5313<div>

5314<h2>

5315How to Maintain Kitchen Organization</h2>

5316

5317

5318<p>

5319The initial organizing of your kitchen cabinets is a great starting point, though regular cleaning and tidying up maintains that sense of organization. Once an area is organized, it&rsquo;s easier to keep organized&mdash;but that doesn&rsquo;t mean maintenance isn&rsquo;t needed.</p>

5320

5321

5322<p>

5323Return your kitchen items to their designated drawer or cabinet after they have been cleaned. Regularly wipe down countertops, shelves, and handles so crumbs and germs don&rsquo;t stick around.</p>

5324

5325

5326<p>

5327By keeping basic tidying rules in place and not simply tossing items wherever you have space, you can easily maintain the organization of your kitchen cabinets and drawers.</p>

5328

5329

5330<p>

5331It&rsquo;s good to do a general clean-out of your kitchen cabinets once a year.</p>

5332

5333

5334<p>

5335By using kitchen cabinet and drawer organization accessories, you can optimize the storage and functionality of your kitchen spaces. With a wide variety of organization tools available, you can truly customize how you organize your kitchen to suit your needs.</p>

5336

5337</div>

5338</div>

5339</div>
